                             10. Rechitsa
                           Washing on Shabbos


A. The Fundamental Gezeira

Chazal forbade bathing with hot water on Shabbos due to concerns about
bathhouse attendants heating water on Shabbos.

Two categories apply, each with different leniencies.


Water Type                            What is Permitted


Mayim she'huchmu m'Erev               Permitted: hands, face, feet. Also individual
Shabbos (heated before                limbs - as long as not majority of body in
Shabbos)                              one session.


Mayim she'huchmu b'Shabbos            Generally forbidden. Exception: situation of
(heated on Shabbos, even              pain - entire body permitted.
permissibly)


Heated on Erev Shabbos but            Status disputed by Acharonim - discussed
completed on Shabbos                  extensively in shiurim


B. Special Cases

Case                                  Ruling


Washing a young child with hot        Subject to discussion - health
water on Shabbos                      considerations may apply


Using hot water in the Mikveh         Discussed in dedicated shiur - see
on Shabbos                            Rechitsa Shiur 3


Cold shower / bath / swimming         Generally permitted - Rechitsa gezeira
                                      applies only to hot water

         1. Oneg Shabbos and Kavod Shabbos

Status of the Obligation

Authority /         Ruling
Position


Oneg & Kavod        Divrei Kabbala (from Yeshaya 58:13) - not Torah-level, but
Shabbos - general   treated with great seriousness. Divrei Sofrim are more
                    severe than Divrei Torah (Shaar Hatsion).


Ramban              Oneg Shabbos may be a Mitzva doraisa - derived from
                    "Shabbos Shabbason / mikra kodesh" in the Torah


Sefer HaChinuch /   Miderabanan
Beis Yosef


Fasting on          Forbidden - mevatel Oneg Shabbos. Even for one hour if
Shabbos             intent is to fast. Certainly forbidden until chatzos.


Counting Toward Shabbos - Zachor

Zachor es Yom       Mitzva to count each day from Shabbos (e.g., "today is the
HaShabbos           first day from Shabbos"). Fulfilled by mentioning the day
                    before Shir Shel Yom.


Buying Food for Shabbos

Ideal practice      Buy food earlier in the week if it will be well-preserved by
(Shammai's          Shabbos and may not be available later. If food is definitely
approach)           available Erev Shabbos, buying then is more clearly
                    l'kavod Shabbos.


Hillel's approach   Waited until Erev Shabbos out of bitachon - only
                    appropriate for one on that level. For everyone else,
                    Shammai's approach is correct.
p. 29820. Various — Part 2
       2. Takanas Ezra - Laundry on Thursday



Core Halacha

The Takana     Ezra decreed that laundry should be done on Thursday, so that
               one enters Shabbos with clean clothing.


Opinion        Position


Magen          Equally acceptable to do laundry on any earlier day of the week
Avraham


Elyah          Davka on Thursday
Rabbah


General        Many Poskim: one does not have to wash all clothing unless it is
rule           dirty


Applies Nowadays?

Most           Yes - applies even though laundry is done far quicker than in the
Poskim         times of the takana


Rav Ovadia     Does not apply nowadays
Yosef


Thursday Night

Rav Karelitz   Takana applies to Thursday night as well


Rav Abba       Does not apply Thursday night. Also: applies only if one does
Shaul          not have a dryer (even with a machine). In time of need, may do
               laundry Erev Shabbos without a dryer.
p. 29920. Various — Part 2
                3. Erev Shabbos Preparations



Getting Up Early / General Preparations

Obligation         One should get up early to begin preparations. Everyone
                   must do some preparations - even talmidei chachamim,
                   even menial tasks, for the sake of Shabbos.


Challah

Traditional        Women would make their own challah on Erev Shabbos.
practice           Biur Halacha: one should not mevatel this minhag.


Nowadays           Rav Abba Shaul: minhag does not apply with same severity.
(bakery challah)   Rav Elyashiv: does not apply if one prefers the bakery
                   challah.


What to Eat on Shabbos

Chashuv food       Eating chashuv (impressive) food fulfils Oneg and Kavod
                   Shabbos, but there is no obligation if one does not enjoy it


Hot food           One should not avoid hot food unless it is harmful


Fish               Inyan to eat fish; but if one does not enjoy it, no need to eat
                   it


Two tavshilin      Inyan to have two cooked dishes at each seudah


Personal Preparation - Washing and Grooming

Washing            Mitzva to wash face, hands, and feet with hot water on Erev
                   Shabbos. Tur: ideally wash whole body. Praiseworthy to go
                   to mikveh.
p. 30020. Various — Part 2
Nails             Mitzva to cut nails on Erev Shabbos (not Sunday -
                  superstition concern). Various minhagim on which fingers to
                  start with.


Hair              If hair is long, should cut it on Erev Shabbos




        4. Travelling and Eating on Erev Shabbos



Case                            Ruling


Travelling on Erev Shabbos      Permitted, but should try to arrive at
                                destination at least one hour before Shabbos
                                starts


Big seudah on Erev              Forbidden unless Seudas Mitzva b'zman (e.g.,
Shabbos                         bris). Even then, ideally begin before chatzos.


Eating until Shabbos            Permitted, but a mitzva not to be kovaya
                                seudah - should not set a regular meal


Erev Shabbos that is Erev       Ideally begin before nine and a half hours into
Yom Tov - Seudah Shlishis       the halachic day


Doing melachah after            Forbidden unless l'sorekh Shabbos
Mincha Ketanah


Store owner                     Should close at least one hour before
                                Shabbos begins
p. 30120. Various — Part 2
                  5. Tosefes Shabbos
                     Adding time to Shabbos




Is There a Chiyuv?

Opinion              Position


Rov Rishonim         Mitzva doraisa to begin Shabbos before it technically
                     starts - halacha follows this view


Rambam               No mitzva doraisa of Tosefes Shabbos


Beis Yosef           Not even a mitzva derabanan
(understanding
Rambam)


Gra (understanding   There is a mitzva derabanan
Rambam)


When Must One Begin Tosefes Shabbos?

Rabbeinu Tam /       Issur melacha begins long after first shekiah (bein
Mechaber approach    hashmashos is ~1 hour after first shekiah). Tosefes
                     Shabbos is before first shekiah.


Mishnah Berurah      Must begin Tosefes Shabbos before the first shekiah


Some Rishonim        Chiyuv is only a kol shehu (tiny amount) before
                     Shabbos begins


Most Rishonim        A significant amount of time before Shabbos begins


How to Accept Tosefes Shabbos
p. 30220. Various — Part 2
Many Rishonim         Suffices to lifrosh mimelacha - stop melacha - with
                      kavannah to fulfil the mitzva


Some Rishonim /       Must verbally acknowledge Shabbos
Mishnah Berurah


Practical ruling      Ideally verbally acknowledge Shabbos (Rav Elyashiv,
                      Rav Wosner also). M'ikar hadin: lifrosh mimelacha
                      suffices.


If davening Mincha    Should lifrosh mimelacha before Mincha if no time to
close to shekiah      verbally bring in Shabbos


Tosefes Shabbos of the Tzibbur

If majority of shul   Minority may not do melacha, but may still daven
accepted Shabbos      Mincha


Multiple shuls in     Bound by the latest shul, not by majority
neighborhood


One shul in one's     Rav Elyashiv: bound by that shul. Rav Abba Shaul:
nusach                unsure.


Family / Wife

When husband          Poskim dispute whether family must stop melacha.
accepts Shabbos       Permitted to do issurei derabanan in bein
                      hashmashos unless tzibbur already accepted.


Tosefes Shabbos at    Obligation exists but no need to have kavannah.
end of Shabbos        Piskei Teshuvos: praiseworthy to intend to fulfil the
                      mitzva.
p. 30320. Various — Part 2
                       6. Hadlakas Neiros
                           Shabbos candles




The Chiyuv

Nature of obligation     Obligatory. Three reasons: (1) Kavod Shabbos, (2)
                         Oneg Shabbos, (3) Shalom Bayis. All three apply in
                         different ways.


Where to light           Must eat where one lights. If very unpleasant to eat
                         there, may eat elsewhere.


How Many Neiros?

Basic obligation         One ner. Accepted halacha: two neiros.


Various minhagim         Some add more (e.g., one per child). A woman may
                         light per her minhag; husband should ideally pay but
                         is not obligated.


The Penalty (Knas)

Forgot to light          Must add one additional ner every Shabbos from
                         then on


When knas applies        Machlokes in various cases - ask a Rav for specific
                         situations


Who Lights?

Primary responsibility   The woman. Good for the man to be involved.


Man living alone         Must light neiros
p. 30420. Various — Part 2
Wife not home          Machlokes whether man should light, or a girl above
                       Bas Mitzvah


Some minhagim          All girls in the home light with a bracha


Blind woman            May light with a bracha. If married, husband should
                       ideally light and say the bracha.


What to Light With

Ideal oil              Olive oil (Mechaber). Some Poskim: regular candles
                       even more ideal (no shema yateh concern).


Electric lights        If cannot light a flame: may use electric lights with a
                       bracha (most Poskim). Rav Auerbach: battery-
                       powered flashlight if possible. Rav Elyashiv: electric
                       or fluorescent bulbs acceptable.


The Bracha - Light First or Bracha First?

Mechaber               Say bracha first, then light


Rama / Ashkenaz        Light first (covering eyes), then say bracha
minhag


Rav Ovadia Yosef       All Sefardim should say bracha first, even if minhag
                       was otherwise


Rav Abba Shaul         May follow one's minhag; if no minhag - bracha first


Men                    Never mekabel Shabbos with the hadlaka regardless
                       of order


Mekabeles Shabbos with the Bracha

Behag                  Woman is mekabeles Shabbos with hadlaka
p. 30520. Various — Part 2
Rosh / Mechaber           Woman is NOT mekabeles Shabbos with hadlaka


Ashkenaz minhag           Woman IS mekabeles Shabbos with the bracha
(Rama)


Special Cases - Away from Home

Case                      Ruling


Man away from home        Fulfils obligation through wife's lighting, unless he
(wife lights at home)     has his own room where he stays and there is
                          sufficient light so he won't stumble.


Different time zones      Poskim dispute whether still exempted
from wife


Wife away from home       Same exemption - husband fulfils through wife's
(husband home)            lighting


Both husband and          Husband is NOT exempted from his obligation
wife away from home


Guests

Guest without own         Must mishtatef b'prutah if eating own food in host's
room, wife not lighting   home
at home


Guest eating host's       Machlokes whether exempted or must mishtatef
food                      b'prutah


Kavua - definition        30 days
(Rav Elyashiv)


Multiple People Lighting in Same Place

Mechaber                  Second person cannot say bracha
p. 30620. Various — Part 2
Rama / Ashkenaz           Second person says a bracha
minhag


Electric lights present   Shvus Yitzchak: second woman cannot say bracha
                          (adds no light). Acharonim debate cases where ner
                          adds very little light.


Electric Lights Already On

Accepted minhag           Light neiros with bracha even when electric lights are
                          on


Ideal practice (Rav       Turn on electric lights immediately before lighting
Elyashiv, Rav             neiros so bracha covers both
Berkovits)


Lighting in a bedroom     Must ensure that without the neiros the room would
                          be dark enough to risk stumbling


Hotel / Hospital

Hotel - cannot light in   Cannot say bracha. May light electric light in
makom achila or           bedroom and say bracha on that.
bedroom


Bathroom light            Poskim debate if bracha may be said


Woman in hospital         Technically need not light if husband lights at home
                          and some light in her room. But many Poskim:
                          should light. Cannot say bracha unless in makom
                          achila or bedroom.


Bachurim in Yeshiva

Obligation                Poskim dispute if bachur needs to mishtatef and if he
                          can light with bracha in his bedroom
p. 30720. Various — Part 2
                           7. Kiddush
                  Friday night and Shabbos morning




The Obligation

Doraisa            Mitzva doraisa to mention (verbally sanctify) Shabbos at its
component          onset - "Zachor es Yom HaShabbos"


Kiddush on wine    Rishonim and Acharonim dispute whether kiddush on wine
                   is doraisa. Most Poskim hold it is miderabanan.


Man motsi wife     Generally no problem - most Poskim permit
who has not
davened Maariv


Timing

When to make       Ideally as soon as he arrives home, unless not hungry
Kiddush


Eating before      Forbidden to eat or drink anything before Kiddush
Kiddush


Children above     Most Poskim: permitted to eat/drink for health. Debate if
chinuch before     permitted for other food.
Kiddush


Covering the Challah

Must cover         Yes - at all Shabbos meals (some lenient for Seudah
challah            Shlishis)


One sitting at     Poskim debate if must cover challah if not drinking the
p. 30820. Various — Part 2
different table     wine


Mezonos at          Poskim debate if must cover mezonos
Kiddush


The Position During Kiddush

Sitting vs.         Different minhagim. Various hiddurim for holding the
standing            Kiddush cup.


Netilas Yadayim     Mechaber: wash after Kiddush (if washed first, make
- before or after   Kiddush on bread). Rama / common Ashkenaz minhag:
Kiddush?            wash first. Mishnah Berurah: follows Mechaber, but bdi
                    eved if washed first - may make Kiddush on wine.
                    Everyone but Mekadesh may wash first even per
                    Mechaber.


The Kiddush Cup

Condition of cup    Must be whole and unblemished. Should use a nice cup.


No proper cup       May use a disposable cup. If none - use the bottle.
available


Size                Must hold at least a reviis. Be strict for shiur of 137 cubic
                    centimeters for night Kiddush.


Filling the cup     Should be filled to the brim. If not possible, may add
                    foreign matter.
p. 30920. Various — Part 2
Wine and Alternatives

Type                     Ruling


Wine vs. grape juice     Ideally use wine. If one prefers grape juice -
                         permitted. Rav Elyashiv: grape juice that can never
                         become wine is pasul for Kiddush; most Poskim
                         disagree.


Red vs. white wine       Mechaber: permitted to use white, but red is
                         preferable unless one prefers white. Ramban: white
                         is pasul bdi eved.


Cooked wine              Mechaber: permitted, uncooked is preferable.
                         Machlokes Rishonim.


Chamar Medinah - for Shabbos Morning Kiddush

Night Kiddush - no       Make Kiddush on bread (not chamar medinah). May
wine available           make on bread even if prefers bread over wine.


Morning Kiddush - no     Use chamar medinah (e.g., whisky). May NOT
wine                     make on bread in the morning.


What qualifies as        Beer, orange juice, whisky: generally yes.
chamar medinah?          Coffee/tea: machlokes. Soda: machlokes. Chazon
                         Ish: nothing qualifies nowadays.


Drinking the Wine

Mekadesh should drink    A maleh lugmav (majority of a reviis)


If only another person   Rishonim dispute. Mechaber: good to be strict but
drank maleh lugmav       yotsi bdi eved.


Combined drinking        If multiple people combined to drink a maleh lugmav
                         together - all are yotsi
p. 31020. Various — Part 2
Kiddush b'Makom Seudah

Ideal                   Meal must be eaten in same place as Kiddush was
                        made


Leaving the house       Should not leave. Bdi eved - fulfils obligation.
between Kiddush and
meal


Hefsek between          Ideally eat immediately. Hefsekim for sake of the
Kiddush and meal        meal are not a problem.


Had to leave after      Does not need to make Kiddush again when he
Kiddush before eating   returns


What Constitutes a Seudah?

Praiseworthy            Eat bread after Kiddush - fulfils all opinions


Accepted minhag         Mezonos after Kiddush


Maaseh kedeirah         Acceptable


Rice                    Poskim debate


Fruit                   Generally insufficient. If weak with no chameshes
                        haminim food - may eat fruit.


Morning Kiddush -       In need, Mekadesh may drink a reviis instead.
maleh lugmav            Others need only a reviis. If necessary even
                        Mekadesh can drink only a reviis.


Saying Kiddush Oneself vs. Hearing It

Ideal                   One person says for all - "b'rov am hadras Melech"


Listener's              Must have daas to be exempted. Acharonim debate
p. 31120. Various — Part 2
requirements             if must also say Amen bdi eved - seems yotsi
                         regardless.


Mekadesh already         Can still motsi others through arvus
fulfilled his chiyuv


One who has not          Rav Auerbach: lenient only in shaas hadchak
accepted Shabbos
motsi others


Morning Kiddush

Nature of obligation     Miderabanan


Content                  Ikar Kiddush is the blessing on wine. Different
                         customs on which pesukim to add.


Standing vs. sitting     Most common minhag: sit. Some stand.


Woman before             Poskim debate
davening - obligated?


Sick person permitted    Must make Kiddush first
to eat before davening
p. 31220. Various — Part 2
                      8. Shabbos Meals
                       Three meals on Shabbos




The Chiyuv

Who is obligated         Men and women - three meals with bread on
                         Shabbos


If cannot eat bread      Exempt from bread but must still eat meals


Amount of bread          Acharonim debate: more than a kebeitzah, or a
                         kezayis


Pas kisnin               Debate on how much pas kisnin to eat to say
                         Hamotsi and Birchas Hamazon


Times of the Three Meals

Meal                     Time


Friday night meal        Can eat until dawn; ideally begin soon after nightfall.
                         May begin from after plag hamincha; some Poskim:
                         eat kezayis of bread after nightfall.


Shabbos morning meal     Most important meal. Should not overeat if it will
                         prevent eating seudah shlishis. Aruch Hashulchan:
                         before chatzos; most Poskim do not hold this
                         strictly.


Seudah Shlishis          Must eat after time of Mincha (some Poskim
                         lenient). Ideally pray Mincha first. Should begin
                         before it gets too late. Preferable to eat meat or fish
                         rather than fruit.
p. 31320. Various — Part 2
Melaveh Malka

Obligation               Mitzva to eat a meal after Shabbos (Melaveh
                         Malka). Most Poskim: women also obligated.


What to eat              Ideally bread. If unable: mezonos or fruit.


Eats kezayis of bread    Some Poskim: fulfils Melaveh Malka. Others:
during seudah shlishis   requires a separate meal.
after nightfall


Minhag                   Keep Shabbos clothes until after Melaveh Malka
p. 31420. Various — Part 2
                  9. Lechem Mishneh
                      Two loaves at Shabbos meals


The Obligation

Magen Avraham                Chiyuv miderabanan


Taz                          Chiyuv midoraisa


Breaking the Loaf

Rashi, Rambam, Tur           Break only one loaf (Mechaber rules this way;
                             Minhag follows Mechaber)


Rashba / Maharshal,          Must break both loaves
Shelah, Gra


Which Loaf to Break?

Friday night                 Mechaber: break the lower loaf


All other meals (Shabbos     Rama: break the higher loaf
day, Yom Tov night)


Bach                         Always break the higher loaf


Magen Avraham                Put the loaf to break on top during Kiddush, then
                             place it lower for Hamotsi


Taz                          Hold lower loaf closer to one's body


Making a roshem (mark)       Poskim dispute whether this is better
before cutting
p. 31520. Various — Part 2
How large a piece to break     Mitzva to break a large piece that will suffice for
                               the entire meal


If One Does Not Have Two Whole Loaves

Have one whole and one         Use one whole + one broken loaf
broken


Only broken loaves             Use two broken loaves


Loaf that broke in two         Connect with toothpick (not visible) - considered
                               shalem. Cannot do with three pieces.


Sliced bread in a closed       NOT considered whole
bag


Special Cases

Loaf one is generally strict   Permitted to use for lechem mishneh
not to eat from


Borrowed loaf (must be         Poskim debate - many are lenient
returned)


Frozen loaf                    Poskim debate - many are lenient
p. 31620. Various — Part 2
                       10. Havdala
               Separating Shabbos from the weekday




Is Havdala Doraisa or Derabanan?

Machlokes Rishonim    Some: doraisa. Others: derabanan. Chazal fixed
                      Havdala both in Shemoneh Esrei ("Atah chonantanu")
                      and on a cup of wine.


Forgot "Atah          Does not need to repeat the Shemoneh Esrei
chonantanu"


Who is Obligated?

Person                Ruling


Women                 Most Rishonim: obligated. Mechaber: brings both
                      opinions; ikar is obligated. Rama/Taz: should not
                      make Havdala for themselves. Bach/Magen
                      Avraham/Mishnah Berurah: women may make
                      Havdala for themselves.


Man making Havdala    Ideally should not. In time of need: permitted.
for woman (already
fulfilled his own)


Woman making          Ideally should not. In time of need: permitted.
Havdala for man


Children (above       Must hear Havdala (may eat first). Debate if child who
chinuch)              went to sleep before end of Shabbos must hear next
                      day.


Man motsi child in    Even if already fulfilled his own chiyuv
p. 31720. Various — Part 2
Havdala


Child motsi adult    Only if adult said "hamavdil" and child has not. If child
                     also said "hamavdil" - machlokes.


Blind person         Obligated in Havdala but cannot say bracha on fire for
                     himself


Onein                May not hear Havdala. After burial - must hear
                     Havdala unless after sunset on Tuesday.


Eating and Drinking Before Havdala

After shekiah        Forbidden to eat or drink anything (except water)
                     before making Havdala


Began eating bread   May continue eating and drinking until he bentches
before shekiah


Began drinking       Must stop at shekiah
before shekiah


Began eating         Poskim debate if may continue
mezonos before
shekiah


Doing Melacha Before Havdala

After nightfall      Forbidden (machlokes if rabbinic or has Torah source)
without Havdala


How to permit        "Baruch hamavdil bein kodesh lechol", "Atah
Melacha              chonantanu" in Shemoneh Esrei, or Havdala on wine -
                     all permit Melacha


Before Kedusha in    Ideal not to do Melacha until after Kedusha of Maariv
Maariv
p. 31820. Various — Part 2
Asking others to do    Permitted even before Havdala
Melacha


Lighting candles       One opinion permits without Havdala; Rama is strict


Zmanim of Havdala

If did not make        Rama: may make until (not including) Tuesday night.
Havdala on Motsei      Sefardi Poskim: debate.
Shabbos


Making Havdala         Mechaber: permits. Mishnah Berurah: only if cannot
before nightfall       make it by Tuesday night.
(onnes)


Making Havdala         Ideally daven Maariv first. In time of need: Havdala
before Maariv          first.




The Havdala Procedure

Element               Halacha


Cup of wine           Should overflow out of the cup. Various minhagim on
                      standing vs. sitting.


Drinking the Havdala Wine

Amount to drink       Must drink a maleh lugmav; ideally drink a reviis


Who drinks            Only one person should drink. If enough wine, others
                      may drink the rest.


Women                 Ideally do not drink the wine. If no man available - a
                      woman should drink.
p. 31920. Various — Part 2
Besamim

Why we smell          To alleviate the loss of the neshama yeseirah at the
besamim               end of Shabbos


Ashkenazim            Always say "borei minei besamim." Ideally use a spice
                      with that bracha.


Sefardim              Say the fitting bracha for the specific spice. Use a
                      hadas.


Fruit with pleasant   May use. Should wait until after making Havdala before
smell                 smelling.


Havdala Candle (Ner)

Mitzva                Mitzva to say bracha on a ner on Motsei Shabbos. May
                      say until alos hashachar.


Women                 Mishnah Berurah: not obligated. Many Poskim: may say
                      the bracha. Debate.


Blind person          Cannot say bracha on the ner. Poskim unsure if can
                      motsi others.


Type of ner           Ideally multi-wicked candle. May use a single flame.
                      Must be lit in a permitted way, for the sake of giving
                      light.


Electric bulb         Poskim debate if bracha may be said


Proximity             Must be close enough to potentially derive benefit from
                      the ner


Bracha before or      Machlokes. Some do both (say bracha and then
after benefit         benefit, and then benefit again) to fulfil both opinions.
p. 32020. Various — Part 2
     11. Kabbalas Shabbos and Tefila


Kabbalas Shabbos

Purpose                  Minhag to say Kabbalas Shabbos as Shabbos
                         enters - primary purpose is Kavod Shabbos


When Shabbos is          "Boi b'kallah" (Lecha Dodi) brings in Shabbos, as
brought in               does Barechu


Tefila Notes

Bracha before Krias      Different ending. Bdi eved - yotsi if said weekday
Shema (Friday night)     bracha.


"Veshamru" before        Most communities say it. Ashkenazim in Eretz
Shemoneh Esrei           Yisrael: do not say it, based on Gra.


Me'eyn Sheva (Magen Avos)

When said                Friday night, after Shemoneh Esrei


Purpose                  Said for those who arrive late to shul - condensed
                         form of the Shabbos Amidah


Shabbos Shacharis Additions

Additions to Shacharis   Various additions to the Shabbos Shacharis service
                         - discussed in shiurim


Chazzan repeating        Practical notes discussed in shiurim (including
Shemoneh Esrei           situation where person should say Shabbos
                         Shemoneh Esrei himself)
